A pip is a dot on the face of a dice which counts as a point of movement or placement.\r\n\r\n‚úì When your turn comes you start by rolling the dice and continue by making the moves.\r\n\r\n‚úì If you roll a double your pips count will be twice the pipsÔøΩÔøΩ sum of the dice.\r\n\r\n‚úì After you roll the dice some top pieces on your triangles, will be highlighted. Then, at that point the triangle turns blue and the places to which you can move next turn green. Tap on any of those green triangles to initiate the move.
